<Rate>5< /Rate><Text>Briar Rose winery was magic üåü

For Labor Day weekend, I wanted to get away somewhere I hadn‚Äôt been before, but was in a short driving distance. I did some googling and found Snow White‚Äôs cottage. I am a HUGE original Disney fan (things from Walt‚Äôs time), so I knew I had to visit.

When we arrived, even the parking lot had a view. You had a gorgeous view of all the vineyards below you, and Briar Rose itself was covered from the outside with this whimsical type of bush. You enter the bush and all of a sudden, you find yourself in Snow White‚Äôs garden, surrounded by her cute squirrel friends, wishing well, and her seven dwarves.

The original quaint cottage was built in the 1970‚Äôs by Disney imagineer Beldon Fields. While working for Disney, Beldon collected bits and pieces of Disney artifacts which made their way into the cottage. Some tiles from Mr. Toads, a rock from Indiana Jones, and a lantern from Haunted Mansion make the grounds so much more special.

Beauty aside, the wine tasting is delicious. We started out with a wonderful cracker and homemade cheese kit while we waited on our wine. We got one red wine tasting, and one white wine tasting before ordering a couple extra glasses to enjoy the scenery a bit longer.

I cannot recommend Briar Rose enough! Delicious wine, knowledgeable staff, and a view to die for. I‚Äôll be coming back to Temecula just to enjoy the winery. üç∑

Want more reviews? < Review>
Our server was Eric. Learned few things while tasting their wines. Why red wine is red? Because of the processing technique: the grape skin is added while the wines is fermenting. That's what gives it a red color. This is also why the red wines have more beneficial properties. Unlike white wines that are processed without grape skin.
Why storing red wine bottles horizontally ? The red wine bottles should be laid flat so that sediment from the wine settles evenly on one side and the cork is submerged to the wine which keeps it moist. Dry corks will make your wine bitter.
Very interesting. It was my first ever experience with wine tasting. The place is quiet and green with roses and old house. I like that seats are outdoor under the trees shade. The only thing was not so pleasant is experience with hostess. Not friendly at all.</Review>

< Text>
Purchased the Groupon, but our server, Brandon, was super cool, giving us double shot tastings. The venue is super cutesie having the same name as Disney's Snow White, "Briar Rose".

If you look hard enough you may find all 7 of the dwarves hiding around the premises. Like Easter Eggs.

It's a small and intimate venue, a great setting for a party of 4-6, but romantic enough for two. The outdoor seating was in beautiful gardens with a variety of sculptures.

We purchased the "Talking Frog" for my cousin and ended up finishing 2 bottles. An interesting wine with some Hefeweizen, flavoring it like a beer.<//Text>

<rate>5</rate>< Text>
I give this hotel a full five stars because there is different variables to consider. Although the location is not favorable to many especially tourist, around the Westlake MacArthur Park area is considered one of the bad areas of town, there are many homeless people which breed drug addicts, possible vandalizing, uncomfortability etc. Nevertheless, the Royal Viking has created a facility that has many deterrents and precautions put in place to protect the property and its patrons. The staff is amazingly courteous, nice, outstanding work ethic and accommodating. No matter what I asked for the gentleman in the front desk was very courteous and retrieved any amenity I requested within their services. We spoke briefly and in the conversation I mentioned I was in the service for 15 years, and he went out of his way to thank me for my service and motivated him to provide excellent customer service to me more so than he was doing before I mentioned my time in the Marines. After 6:00 p.m. there is a security guard protecting the property which includes customers safety, vehicles and property. The security guard is very aggressive with anyone that is not a customer so therefore it deters the bad elements. Also, after 6:00 p.m. along with security they have a gated community which the access code is given to customers, and if you lose the number the security guard will gladly assist you and allow you in after verification. Which is a great precaution for the safety of the customers. I had a great time and felt safe while I was asleep with my family.<//Text>

< Text>
Ok so first of all this is a motel - if you want a five star hotel (not be be confused with a five star google reviewed MO-tel) then go elsewhere. We requested a room with the parquet floor, which was much cleaner than a room with a carpet I imagine. I would recommend recommending this floor type. The gentleman at the front desk was incredibly nice and helpful. As were the cleaning staff, who let us leave the room a tad late because something came up on our end. (Never count on getting a late check-out until day of departure, it all depends on how much work the cleaning staff has to do, if any). As for the neighborhood, it's a short walk to 6th and Alvarado street. Some people on Google reviews call it "dangerous." I think what these reviewers actually mean is that this motel located in a majority minority neighborhood, which perhaps makes them uncomfortable. Get over it ya'll and go take a walk around to find some fun open-air markets and treat yourself to some delicious Korean, Salvadoran, or Oaxacan food, among other authentic cuisines.< /Text>

Visited Merryvale Vineyards in St. Helena, CA on July 26th with friends from Tucson. Shelby was our wine educator. She was fabulous. Fun, personable, knew her stuff.

The last time I smogged a car it costed me just below $30.00 and I assumed it would cost more now but I was pleasantly surprised that it was $29.95 + Certificate fee ($8.25, I beleive)...which left me with a bill of $38.20!!! Granted I would have loved to spend less than $30 but that was over three years ago.
When I walked it, I was greeted by a soft spoken gentleman. He simply asked me how I heard about his business, I told him Google Maps and he told me that it would be the special price + Certificate fee, I told him that would be great. I pulled my new car in to the bay and he began the smog check. I simply hung out with him during the maybe 5 minutes it took him to complete everything. He was very professional, polite, and was very resectful of my vehicle (which is very important to me).
Overall I would highly recommend coming here to get your smog done at an extremely fair cost, very quick service, have your vehicle treated well, and some great customer service</review>< Date>

<text>Solid place for a good meal. While in San Diego, we found a Woodranch restaurant right next to our hotel in Mission Valley.

We missed the food in this restaurant as the Woodranch in Arcadia had shut its door as a victim of the pandemic. Their BBQ baby back ribs are amazing. The ribs are so tender and the meat just falls off the bones. The Natalie Salad is also one of my favorites. The salad dressing for this salad is best with vinaigrette.

The buttery garlic roll is also a reason that I missed the this restaurant. This fluffy tasty bread is my favorite. I would be fine if I can just only eat this roll without getting any other food.

I need to research a bit to find out where are remaining Woodranch restaurants in LA.< /text>< Time>

<rate>5< /rate><Review>This was my very first time in Wood Ranch. Always smells so good walking by, so I decided to try it today.  Greeted promptly and seated. My server was prompt too, handing me the menu and taking my drink order.  Also brought some complimentary butter garlic rolls, which were so delicious!
For the meal I order their combo which comes with a your choice of 2 or 3 items and one side. I chose the chicken breast, BBQ ribs (5 bones,) and beef brisket.  Also a side of Mac and cheese.

<Text>Stopped in for a bite and to check it out as I seen the sign from my River Run run....(odd to say....)
Waiter (Mikey, as it stated on my receipt) was friendly, attentive, and knowledgeable.
Ordered the Appetizer Onion skins. Holy Moly! It is enough for 4 people! Tasted good though.
Ordered the 8oz Filet with side of grilled Asparagus. Food was made exactly as I asked (I am not high maintenance, hm!)
I was glad they have raw horseradish but I must say it was quite tame...kind of like to have my nose and eyes rung by horse radish though. Would have been nice to have choice of creamy version or both.
Anyway, also ordered coffee, which they made a new pot (Oh Sank you Doctor!), also had a two glasses of Arnold Palmer, both of which tasted the same (I was grateful).

<Time>1579233235310<//Time><Rating>4</Rating>< Review>
Stopped in for a bite and to check it out as I seen the sign from my River Run run....(odd to say....)
Waiter (Mikey, as it stated on my receipt) was friendly, attentive, and knowledgeable.
Ordered the Appetizer Onion skins. Holy Moly! It is enough for 4 people! Tasted good though.
Ordered the 8oz Filet with side of grilled Asparagus. Food was made exactly as I asked (I am not high maintenance, hm!)
I was glad they have raw horseradish but I must say it was quite tame...kind of like to have my nose and eyes rung by horse radish though. Would have been nice to have choice of creamy version or both.
Anyway, also ordered coffee, which they made a new pot (Oh Sank you Doctor!), also had a two glasses of Arnold Palmer, both of which tasted the same (I was grateful).
Overall, will return, and share with friends about this place. I think there are a few other items I intend to try on BBQ side....
BTW, was this location that used to be (back in the day) a Sports bar...Randy Johnson or such? Anyhoo, chow!</Review>

Was passing by from fashion valley and happened to see it as my husband was driving. The ambiance is very nice here, really does smell of wood as tou come in. Full of booth's which i like as my toddler hates high chairs right now.
Now as to the food, they give you some pretty bomb garlic bread:) i ordered the brisket w mac n cheese and fries (which i shared w my daughter) and my husband ordered the baby back ribs w corn on the cob and asparagus. My brisket was very flavorful and tender! My husband wasn't too impressed w ribs, however. Ribs weren't tender. With all that being said- we would come here again. 07/18/16:  4.5 out of 5 - We came here a little after 8pm for a table of 17 after a family funeral event.  Admittedly, we needed to wind down.

Very welcoming, open concept ambiance.
The bar seating not only has purse hooks which are always handy, but it is also lit from underneath and has electric outlets every few feet to accomodate phone or laptop chargers.

Known for years for their mouth-watering BBQ, Wood Ranch will satisfy your hankering for pulled pork or tender brisket.
Happy hour pricing on craft beers and appetizers make this a great place to chill after work.</review>

<Time>1551925833207</Time><rate>4< /rate>< Text>
Went there for lunch on a Sunday. The waitress was attentive, quick, friendly, and professional.  The manager, not so much.  I told him the macaroni was undercooked and he got this snarky attitude and replied "we make our macaroni and cheese differently...it's al dente".  He should learn what "al dente" means before using the term.  It DOES NOT mean hard, gritty, starchy in the pasta core.  I've been to Italy, it's their word, and they certainly don't make it the way our macaroni was served that day.  The waitress, however, save the day.  Chipper as always, she offered an alternative.  We didn't take it, but appreciated her courtesy.  The rest of the food was outstanding.  The Farm House salad was yummy!  Loved the dressing.  The meat was perfectly cooked and seasoned.  The sauce was outstanding!  Nice atmosphere too.</Text>

< Text>
Great bbq!

My wife and I come here for causal dinner dates. We can have an adult meal and not feel we have to pay through the nose and get totaly dresses up. Though we seen families here all the time.

Usally it's so busy we sit in the bar so make a reservation or come early. But we always had good service in the bar as we had at a table.

We are fans of the brisket and tri tip. The tri tip salad is also really good if you want something a little less meat and more greens. Also the garlic rolls are wonderful. My wife is a huge fan of their beans. She usally can't eat it all and says the beans reheat really well the next day.

Also you can watch the cooks cut up all the ribs and meat from a "fish tank" like window if you are in to that kind of thing.< /Text>
